Check Endpoint Implementation Comparison\\n\\n### Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)\\n\\n**Endpoints:**\\n- `/healthz` - liveness/general health\\n- `/livez` - liveness (subset of readiness checks)\\n- `/readyz` - readiness (when ready to serve traffic)\\n\\n**Implementation** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz/healthz.go`):\\nKubernetes has a comprehensive health check framework with pluggable health checkers. The endpoints are registered via `InstallHandler()`, `InstallLivezHandler()`, and `InstallReadyzHandler()` functions in the healthz package. Each endpoint supports multiple health checks that can be selectively excluded via query parameters (e.g., `/healthz?exclude=etcd`).\\n\\n**Checks Performed:**\\n1. **Ping check** - Basic liveness (always passes)\\n2. **Log check** - Verifies logging is not blocked\\n3. **Informer sync check** - Readyz only, ensures all Kubernetes informers have synced\\n4. **Shutdown check** - Detects graceful shutdown state\\n5. **etcd health checks** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/etcd.go`):\\n   - etcd-healthiness: Tests basic etcd connectivity\\n   - etcd-readiness: Tests if etcd is ready for API operations\\n   - Supports multiple etcd server configurations with per-server health checks\\n6. **API service availability checks** - Custom checks for API service discovery\\n7. **Post-start hook checks** - Tracks completion of post-start initialization hooks\\n\\n**Key Features:**\\n- Grouped health checks (e.g., etcd checks are grouped under \\\"etcd\\\" group for bulk exclusion)\\n- Individual endpoint access: `/readyz/ping`, `/readyz/etcd-readiness`, etc.\\n- Verbose output: `/readyz?verbose=1` shows individual check results\\n- Prometheus SLI integration for observability\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus)\\n\\n**Endpoints:**\\n- `/-/healthy` - Health check (always returns 200 OK)\\n- `/-/ready` - Readiness check (depends on server state)\\n\\n**Implementation** (`web/web.go`):\\nPrometheus uses a simple state-machine based health model. The web Handler maintains a `ready` field using atomic operations with three states: `NotReady`, `Ready`, and `Stopping`. The `/-/healthy` endpoint always responds with 200 OK to indicate the HTTP server is running. The `/-/ready` endpoint uses the `testReady()` method (aliased as `readyf` when registering routes) to check the current ready state.\\n\\n**Checks Performed:**\\n1. **HTTP server liveness** - `/-/healthy` always returns 200 OK with message \\\"{AppName} is Healthy\\\"\\n2. **TSDB readiness** - `/-/ready` checks the internal ready status:\\n   - Returns 200 OK if `Ready`\\n   - Returns 503 Service Unavailable with appropriate state if `NotReady` or `Stopping`\\n   - Sets `X-Prometheus-Stopping: true` header during graceful shutdown\\n   - Sets `X-Prometheus-Stopping: false` during normal NotReady state\\n\\n**State Transitions:**\\n- Server starts in `NotReady` state\\n- Transitions to `Ready` when TSDB and storage are initialized\\n- Transitions to `Stopping` when shutdown signal is received\\n\\n**Configuration:**\\nThe ready status is managed via `SetReady()` method, allowing the main Prometheus application to coordinate readiness with storage initialization. The `testReady()` handler wraps HTTP handlers to enforce the readiness check.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Endpoints:**\\n- `/healthz` - Simple health check (always returns 200 OK)\\n- `/api/health` - Comprehensive health check with database status\\n- `/readyz` - Proxied to Kubernetes-compatible endpoint via apiserver service\\n\\n**Implementation:**\\n\\n**Simple Health (`pkg/api/http_server.go` - `healthzHandler`):**\\nThe `/healthz` endpoint simply returns HTTP 200 with message \\\"Ok\\\" if the web server is running. No dependencies are checked; it's a pure liveness indicator.\\n\\n**Comprehensive Health (`pkg/api/http_server.go` - `apiHealthHandler`):**\\nThe `/api/health` endpoint checks database connectivity and returns:\\n- HTTP 200 with database status \\\"ok\\\" if healthy\\n- HTTP 503 (Service Unavailable) with database status \\\"failing\\\" if database is inaccessible\\n- Response includes version, commit, and enterprise commit information (when not anonymized)\\n\\n**Database Health Check** (`pkg/api/health.go` - `databaseHealthy()`):\\n1. Checks cache for recent health status (5-second TTL)\\n2. Executes `SELECT 1` query via `SQLStore.WithDbSession()` to verify database connectivity\\n3. Caches result for 5 seconds to reduce database load\\n4.
